lt_cv_sys_global_symbol_to_cdecl='sed -n -e '\''s/^T .* \(.*\)$/extern int \1();/p'\'' -e '\''s/^[ABCDGIRSTW][ABCDGIRSTW]* .* \(.*\)$/extern char \1;/p'\'''
